        function generateAllInputs() {

            const visualHook = document.getElementById('visualHook').value.trim();

            const filmIdea = document.getElementById('filmIdea').value.trim();

            const beginning = document.getElementById('beginning').value.trim();
            const middle = document.getElementById('middle').value.trim();
            const ending = document.getElementById('ending').value.trim();

            document.getElementById('outputSection').classList.add('show');
        }

    <script>
        function generateAllInputs() {
            const highConcept = document.getElementById('highConcept').value.trim();
            const logline = document.getElementById('logline').value.trim();
            const coreConflict = document.getElementById('coreConflict').value.trim();
            const visualHook = document.getElementById('visualHook').value.trim();

            const filmIdea = document.getElementById('filmIdea').value.trim();
            const sceneCount = document.getElementById('sceneCount').value;
            const beginning = document.getElementById('beginning').value.trim();
            const middle = document.getElementById('middle').value.trim();
            const ending = document.getElementById('ending').value.trim();
            const charA = document.getElementById('charA').value.trim();
            const charB = document.getElementById('charB').value.trim();
            const charC = document.getElementById('charC').value.trim();

            const videoStyles = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.video-style:checked'))
                .map(cb => cb.value);

            if (!highConcept || !logline || !coreConflict || !visualHook ||
                !filmIdea || !beginning || !middle || !ending || !charA || !charB || !charC) {
                alert('âš ï¸ Please fill all required fields (Section 0, 1, 2)!');
                return;
            }

            let output = `SECTION_0_IDEA:\n`;
            output += `HIGH_CONCEPT: ${highConcept}\n`;
            output += `LOGLINE: ${logline}\n`;
            output += `CORE_CONFLICT: ${coreConflict}\n`;
            output += `VISUAL_HOOK: ${visualHook}\n\n`;

            output += `SECTION_1_FILM_STRUCTURE:\n`;
            output += `FILM_IDEA: ${filmIdea}\n`;
            output += `SCENE_COUNT: ${sceneCount}\n`;
            output += `BEGINNING: ${beginning}\n`;
            output += `MIDDLE: ${middle}\n`;
            output += `ENDING: ${ending}\n\n`;

            output += `SECTION_2_CHARACTERS:\n`;
            output += `CHARACTER_A: ${charA}\n`;

import google.generativeai as gen

API_KEYS = [
    "KEY1", "KEY2", "KEY3", "KEY4", "KEY5",
    "KEY6", "KEY7", "KEY8", "KEY9", "KEY10"
]

current_key = 0

def switch_key():
    global current_key
    current_key = (current_key + 1) % len(API_KEYS)
    gen.configure(api_key=API_KEYS[current_key])
    print(f"ğŸ”„ Switched to API key #{current_key+1}")

def ask_gemini(prompt):
    global current_key
    
    for attempt in range(len(API_KEYS)):
        try:
            gen.configure(api_key=API_KEYS[current_key])
            model = gen.GenerativeModel("gemini-1.5-flash")
            response = model.generate_content(prompt)
            return response.text

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"ğŸš§ Key #{current_key+1} quota exceeded â†’ switching...")

    raise Exception("âŒ All API keys exceeded quota!")

import google.generativeai as gen

# =========================
# 1) LOAD API KEYS
# =========================
def load_api_keys(path="api_keys.txt"):
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        keys = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]
    if not keys:
        raise Exception("âŒ No API keys found in api_keys.txt")
    return keys

API_KEYS = load_api_keys()
current_key = 0

def switch_key():
    """Switch to next API key in list."""
    global current_key
    current_key = (current_key + 1) % len(API_KEYS)
    gen.configure(api_key=API_KEYS[current_key])
    print(f"ğŸ”„ Switched to API key #{current_key+1}")

# =========================
# 2) GEMINI CALL
# =========================
def ask_gemini(prompt):
    global current_key
    
    for _ in range(len(API_KEYS)):
        try:
            gen.configure(api_key=API_KEYS[current_key])
            model = gen.GenerativeModel("gemini-1.5-flash")

            response = model.generate_content(prompt)
            return response.text.strip()

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âš ï¸ Key #{current_key+1} quota exceeded â†’ switching key...")
            switch_key()

    raise Exception("âŒ All API keys are exhausted!")

# =========================
# 3) LOAD SCENES
# =========================
def load_scenes(path="scenes.txt"):
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        text = f.read()

    scenes = text.split("Scene ")
    result = []

    for s in scenes[1:]:
        number = s.split(":", 1)[0].strip()
        content = s[len(number)+1:].strip()
        result.append(f"Scene {number}: {content}")

    return result

scenes = load_scenes()

# =========================
# 4) JSON TEMPLATE
# =========================
JSON_TEMPLATE = """
Convert the following scene into ONE SINGLE LINE JSON using EXACTLY this structure:

{"scene_number":1,"scene_title":"[Short title]","character":{"name":"[Main character]","appearance":"[Appearance]","emotions":{"primary":"[Primary emotion]","secondary":"[Secondary emotion]"},"voice_tone":"[Voice tone]"},"setting":{"location":"[Place]","environment":"[Environment]","time":"[Day/Night]"},"cinematic":{"camera":"[Camera movement]","lighting":"[Lighting]","mood":"[Mood]","style":"Cinematic 8K realistic","effects":"[Effects]","sound":"[Sound]"},"dialogue":{"characters":[{"speaker":"[Speaker]","line":"[Line]"}]},"action_block":{"length":"150-200 words","content":"[Action scene]"}}

SCENE:
"""

# =========================
# 5) PROCESS & SAVE OUTPUT
# =========================
OUTPUT_FILE = "output_prompts.txt"

with open(OUTPUT_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8") as out:
    for i, scene in enumerate(scenes, start=1):
        print(f"â³ Processing Scene {i}/{len(scenes)} ...")

        prompt = JSON_TEMPLATE + scene
        json_output = ask_gemini(prompt)

        # Always one JSON per line
        out.write(json_output + "\n")

print(f"\nâœ… DONE! Saved {len(scenes)} prompts â†’ {OUTPUT_FILE}")

import google.generativeai as gen

API_KEYS_FILE = "api_keys.txt"
SCENES_FILE = "scenes.txt"
OUTPUT_FILE = "output_prompts.txt"

# ========== 1. LOAD API KEYS ==========

def load_api_keys(path=API_KEYS_FILE):
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        keys = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]
    if not keys:
        raise Exception("âŒ KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y API key trong api_keys.txt")
    return keys

API_KEYS = load_api_keys()
current_key_index = 0

def set_current_key():
    gen.configure(api_key=API_KEYS[current_key_index])
    print(f"ğŸ”‘ Äang dÃ¹ng API key #{current_key_index+1}")

set_current_key()

def switch_key():
    global current_key_index
    current_key_index = (current_key_index + 1) % len(API_KEYS)
    set_current_key()

# ========== 2. LOAD SCENES ==========

def load_scenes(path=SCENES_FILE):
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        text = f.read().strip()

    # TÃ¡ch cáº£nh theo "Scene X:"
    blocks = []
    raw = text.split("Scene ")
    for part in raw[1:]:
        # láº¥y sá»‘ cáº£nh
        num, rest = part.split(":", 1)
        num = num.strip()
        content = rest.strip()
        blocks.append(f"Scene {num}: {content}")
    return blocks

scenes = load_scenes()
print(f"ğŸ“š ÄÃ£ náº¡p {len(scenes)} cáº£nh tá»« {SCENES_FILE}")

# ========== 3. PROMPT TEMPLATE (NODE 2 BASIC) ==========

PROMPT_TEMPLATE = """
You are a cinematic formatter.
Convert the following scene into ONE SINGLE LINE JSON, EXACTLY in this structure:

{"scene_number":1,"scene_title":"[Short title]","character":{"name":"[Main character]","appearance":"[Appearance]","emotions":{"primary":"[Primary emotion]","secondary":"[Secondary emotion]"},"voice_tone":"[Voice tone]"},"setting":{"location":"[Place]","environment":"[Environment]","time":"[Day/Night]"},"cinematic":{"camera":"[Camera shot + movement]","lighting":"[Lighting]","mood":"[Mood]","style":"Cinematic 8K realistic","effects":"[Effects]","sound":"[Ambience]"},"dialogue":{"characters":[{"speaker":"[Speaker]","line":"[Dialogue line]"}]},"action_block":{"length":"150-200 words","content":"[Cinematic action description]"}}

RULES:
- Return ONLY valid JSON.
- JSON MUST be ONE SINGLE LINE (no line breaks).
- Infer missing details logically.
- action_block MUST be 150-200 words.

SCENE:
\"\"\"{scene}\"\"\"
"""

# ========== 4. Gá»ŒI GEMINI Vá»šI XOAY API ==========

def call_gemini(prompt: str) -> str:
    """Gá»i Gemini, náº¿u háº¿t quota thÃ¬ chuyá»ƒn key khÃ¡c."""
    global current_key_index

    for _ in range(len(API_KEYS)):
        try:
            model = gen.GenerativeModel("gemini-1.5-flash")
            resp = model.generate_content(prompt)
            text = resp.text.strip()

            # Ã©p vá» 1 dÃ²ng
            one_line = " ".join(text.splitlines()).strip()
            return one_line

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âš ï¸ Lá»—i / háº¿t quota vá»›i key #{current_key_index+1}: {e}")
            print("ğŸ”„ Äá»•i sang API key tiáº¿p theo...")
            switch_key()

    raise Exception("âŒ Táº¥t cáº£ API key Ä‘á»u lá»—i hoáº·c háº¿t quota.")

# ========== 5. Xá»¬ LÃ Tá»ªNG Cáº¢NH & LÆ¯U RA FILE ==========

def main():
    with open(OUTPUT_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8") as out_f:
        for idx, scene in enumerate(scenes, start=1):
            print(f"â³ Äang xá»­ lÃ½ cáº£nh {idx}/{len(scenes)}...")

            full_prompt = PROMPT_TEMPLATE.format(scene=scene)
            json_line = call_gemini(full_prompt)

            # Ghi má»—i prompt = 1 dÃ²ng
            out_f.write(json_line + "\n")

    print(f"\nâœ… Xong! ÄÃ£ lÆ°u {len(scenes)} prompt vÃ o {OUTPUT_FILE}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import google.generativeai as gen

API_KEYS_FILE = "api_keys.txt"
SCENES_FILE = "scenes.txt"
OUTPUT_FILE = "output_prompts.txt"

# ========== 1. LOAD API KEYS ==========

def load_api_keys(path=API_KEYS_FILE):
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        keys = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]
    if not keys:
        raise Exception("âŒ KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y API key trong api_keys.txt")
    return keys

API_KEYS = load_api_keys()
current_key_index = 0

def set_current_key():
    gen.configure(api_key=API_KEYS[current_key_index])
    print(f"ğŸ”‘ Äang dÃ¹ng API key #{current_key_index+1}")

set_current_key()

def switch_key():
    global current_key_index
    current_key_index = (current_key_index + 1) % len(API_KEYS)
    set_current_key()

# ========== 2. LOAD SCENES ==========

def load_scenes(path=SCENES_FILE):
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        text = f.read().strip()

    blocks = []
    raw = text.split("Scene ")
    for part in raw[1:]:
        num, rest = part.split(":", 1)
        num = num.strip()
        content = rest.strip()
        blocks.append(f"Scene {num}: {content}")
    return blocks

scenes = load_scenes()
print(f"ğŸ“š ÄÃ£ náº¡p {len(scenes)} cáº£nh tá»« {SCENES_FILE}")

# ========== 3. PROMPT TEMPLATE (ESCAPED JSON) ==========

PROMPT_TEMPLATE = """
You are a cinematic formatter.
Convert the following scene into ONE SINGLE LINE JSON, EXACTLY in this structure:

{{"scene_number":1,
"scene_title":"[Short title]",
"character":{{"name":"[Main character]","appearance":"[Appearance]",
"emotions":{{"primary":"[Primary emotion]","secondary":"[Secondary emotion]"}},
"voice_tone":"[Voice tone]"}},
"setting":{{"location":"[Place]","environment":"[Environment]","time":"[Day/Night]"}},
"cinematic":{{"camera":"[Camera shot + movement]","lighting":"[Lighting]","mood":"[Mood]",
"style":"Cinematic 8K realistic","effects":"[Effects]","sound":"[Ambience]"}},
"dialogue":{{"characters":[{{"speaker":"[Speaker]","line":"[Dialogue line]"}}]}},
"action_block":{{"length":"150-200 words","content":"[Cinematic action description]"}}}}

RULES:
- Return ONLY valid JSON.
- JSON MUST be ONE SINGLE LINE (no line breaks).
- Infer missing details logically.
- action_block MUST be 150-200 words.

SCENE:
\"\"\"{scene}\"\"\"
"""

# ========== 4. Gá»ŒI GEMINI ==========

def call_gemini(prompt: str) -> str:
    global current_key_index

    for _ in range(len(API_KEYS)):
        try:
            model = gen.GenerativeModel("gemini-1.5-flash")
            resp = model.generate_content(prompt)
            text = resp.text.strip()

            # Ã©p vá» 1 dÃ²ng
            one_line = " ".join(text.splitlines()).strip()
            return one_line

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âš ï¸ Lá»—i key #{current_key_index+1}: {e}")
            print("ğŸ”„ Äá»•i sang API key tiáº¿p theo...")
            switch_key()

    raise Exception("âŒ Táº¥t cáº£ API key Ä‘á»u lá»—i hoáº·c háº¿t quota.")

# ========== 5. CHáº Y TOÃ€N Bá»˜ ==========

def main():
    with open(OUTPUT_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8") as out_f:
        for idx, scene in enumerate(scenes, start=1):
            print(f"â³ Äang xá»­ lÃ½ cáº£nh {idx}/{len(scenes)}...")

            full_prompt = PROMPT_TEMPLATE.format(scene=scene)
            json_line = call_gemini(full_prompt)

            out_f.write(json_line + "\n")

    print(f"\nâœ… Xong! ÄÃ£ lÆ°u {len(scenes)} prompt vÃ o {OUTPUT_FILE}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

        content = rest.strip()
        blocks.append(f"Scene {num}: {content}")
    return blocks

import google.generativeai as gen

API_KEYS_FILE = "api_keys.txt"
SCENES_FILE = "scenes.txt"
OUTPUT_FILE = "output_prompts.txt"

# ========== 1. LOAD API KEYS ==========

def load_api_keys(path=API_KEYS_FILE):
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        keys = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]
    if not keys:
        raise Exception("âŒ KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y API key trong api_keys.txt")
    return keys

API_KEYS = load_api_keys()
current_key_index = 0

def set_current_key():
    gen.configure(api_key=API_KEYS[current_key_index])
    print(f"ğŸ”‘ Äang dÃ¹ng API key #{current_key_index+1}")

set_current_key()

def switch_key():
    global current_key_index
    current_key_index = (current_key_index + 1) % len(API_KEYS)
    set_current_key()

# ========== 2. LOAD SCENES ==========

def load_scenes(path=SCENES_FILE):
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        text = f.read().strip()

    blocks = []
    raw = text.split("Scene ")
    for part in raw[1:]:
        num, rest = part.split(":", 1)
        num = num.strip()
        content = rest.strip()
        blocks.append(f"Scene {num}: {content}")
    return blocks

scenes = load_scenes()
print(f"ğŸ“š ÄÃ£ náº¡p {len(scenes)} cáº£nh tá»« {SCENES_FILE}")

# ========== 3. PROMPT TEMPLATE (KHÃ”NG DÃ™NG .format) ==========

PROMPT_TEMPLATE = """
You are a cinematic formatter.
Convert the following scene into ONE SINGLE LINE JSON, EXACTLY in this structure:

{"scene_number":1,"scene_title":"[Short title]","character":{"name":"[Main character]","appearance":"[Appearance]","emotions":{"primary":"[Primary emotion]","secondary":"[Secondary emotion]"},"voice_tone":"[Voice tone]"},"setting":{"location":"[Place]","environment":"[Environment]","time":"[Day/Night]"},"cinematic":{"camera":"[Camera shot + movement]","lighting":"[Lighting]","mood":"[Mood]","style":"Cinematic 8K realistic","effects":"[Effects]","sound":"[Ambience]"},"dialogue":{"characters":[{"speaker":"[Speaker]","line":"[Dialogue line]"}]},"action_block":{"length":"150-200 words","content":"[Cinematic action description]"}}

RULES:
- Return ONLY valid JSON.
- JSON MUST be ONE SINGLE LINE (no line breaks).
- Infer missing details logically.
- action_block MUST be 150-200 words.

SCENE:
\"\"\"<<SCENE>>\"\"\"
"""

# ========== 4. Gá»ŒI GEMINI ==========

def call_gemini(prompt: str) -> str:
    global current_key_index

    for _ in range(len(API_KEYS)):
        try:
            model = gen.GenerativeModel("gemini-1.5-flash")
            resp = model.generate_content(prompt)
            text = resp.text.strip()

            # Ã©p vá» 1 dÃ²ng
            one_line = " ".join(text.splitlines()).strip()
            return one_line

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âš ï¸ Lá»—i / háº¿t quota vá»›i key #{current_key_index+1}: {e}")
            print("ğŸ”„ Äá»•i sang API key tiáº¿p theo...")
            switch_key()

    raise Exception("âŒ Táº¥t cáº£ API key Ä‘á»u lá»—i hoáº·c háº¿t quota.")

# ========== 5. CHáº Y Tá»ªNG Cáº¢NH & LÆ¯U RA FILE ==========

def main():
    if not scenes:
        print("âš ï¸ KhÃ´ng cÃ³ cáº£nh nÃ o trong scenes.txt")
        return

    with open(OUTPUT_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8") as out_f:
        for idx, scene in enumerate(scenes, start=1):
            print(f"â³ Äang xá»­ lÃ½ cáº£nh {idx}/{len(scenes)}...")

            full_prompt = PROMPT_TEMPLATE.replace("<<SCENE>>", scene)
            json_line = call_gemini(full_prompt)

            out_f.write(json_line + "\n")

    print(f"\nâœ… Xong! ÄÃ£ lÆ°u {len(scenes)} prompt vÃ o {OUTPUT_FILE}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import google.generativeai as gen

# ==============================
# Cáº¤U HÃŒNH TÃŠN FILE
# ==============================

API_KEYS_FILE = "api_keys.txt"        # Má»—i dÃ²ng 1 API key
SCENES_FILE = "scenes.txt"            # Chá»©a cÃ¡c cáº£nh: Scene 1: ..., Scene 2: ...
OUTPUT_FILE = "output_prompts.txt"    # Má»—i dÃ²ng 1 JSON prompt


# ==============================
# 1. LOAD API KEYS
# ==============================

def load_api_keys(path: str = API_KEYS_FILE):
    """Äá»c danh sÃ¡ch API key (má»—i dÃ²ng 1 key)."""
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        keys = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]
    if not keys:
        raise Exception("âŒ KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y API key nÃ o trong api_keys.txt")
    return keys


API_KEYS = load_api_keys()
current_key_index = 0


def set_current_key():
    """Cáº¥u hÃ¬nh API key hiá»‡n táº¡i cho Gemini."""
    gen.configure(api_key=API_KEYS[current_key_index])
    print(f"ğŸ”‘ Äang dÃ¹ng API key #{current_key_index + 1}")


set_current_key()


def switch_key():
    """Äá»•i sang API key káº¿ tiáº¿p khi key hiá»‡n táº¡i lá»—i / háº¿t quota."""
    global current_key_index
    current_key_index = (current_key_index + 1) % len(API_KEYS)
    set_current_key()


# ==============================
# 2. LOAD SCENES
# ==============================

def load_scenes(path: str = SCENES_FILE):
    """
    Äá»c file scenes.txt vÃ  tÃ¡ch thÃ nh tá»«ng cáº£nh.
    YÃªu cáº§u format:
        Scene 1: ...
        
        Scene 2: ...
        ...
    """
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        text = f.read().strip()

    if not text:
        return []

    blocks = []
    parts = text.split("Scene ")
    for part in parts[1:]:
        # part dáº¡ng: "1: ná»™i dung..." hoáº·c "2: ná»™i dung..."
        if ":" not in part:
            continue
        num, rest = part.split(":", 1)
        num = num.strip()
        content = rest.strip()
        if not content:
            continue
        blocks.append(f"Scene {num}: {content}")

    return blocks


scenes = load_scenes()
print(f"ğŸ“š ÄÃ£ náº¡p {len(scenes)} cáº£nh tá»« {SCENES_FILE}")


# ==============================
# 3. PROMPT TEMPLATE
# ==============================

# DÃ¹ng placeholder <<SCENE>> Ä‘á»ƒ trÃ¡nh lá»—i .format vá»›i dáº¥u {}
PROMPT_TEMPLATE = """
You are a cinematic formatter.
Convert the following scene into ONE SINGLE LINE JSON, EXACTLY in this structure:

{"scene_number":1,"scene_title":"[Short title]","character":{"name":"[Main character]","appearance":"[Appearance]","emotions":{"primary":"[Primary emotion]","secondary":"[Secondary emotion]"},"voice_tone":"[Voice tone]"},"setting":{"location":"[Place]","environment":"[Environment]","time":"[Day/Night]"},"cinematic":{"camera":"[Camera shot + movement]","lighting":"[Lighting]","mood":"[Mood]","style":"Cinematic 8K realistic","effects":"[Effects]","sound":"[Ambience]"},"dialogue":{"characters":[{"speaker":"[Speaker]","line":"[Dialogue line]"}]},"action_block":{"length":"150-200 words","content":"[Cinematic action description]"}}

RULES:
- Return ONLY valid JSON.
- JSON MUST be ONE SINGLE LINE (no line breaks).
- Infer missing details logically.
- action_block MUST be 150-200 words.

SCENE:
\"\"\"<<SCENE>>\"\"\"
"""


# ==============================
# 4. Gá»ŒI GEMINI Vá»šI XOAY API
# ==============================

def call_gemini(prompt: str) -> str:
    """
    Gá»i Gemini vá»›i ná»™i dung prompt.
    Náº¿u 1 API key lá»—i / háº¿t quota â†’ tá»± Ä‘á»™ng Ä‘á»•i sang API key khÃ¡c.
    """
    global current_key_index

    for _ in range(len(API_KEYS)):
        try:
            # DÃ¹ng Ä‘Ãºng model mÃ  báº¡n Ä‘ang dÃ¹ng trong tool: models/gemini-2.5-flash
            model = gen.GenerativeModel("models/gemini-2.5-flash")
            resp = model.generate_content(prompt)

            # Láº¥y text, xoÃ¡ xuá»‘ng dÃ²ng â†’ Ã©p thÃ nh 1 dÃ²ng
            text = (resp.text or "").strip()
            one_line = " ".join(text.splitlines()).strip()
            return one_line

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âš ï¸ Lá»—i vá»›i key #{current_key_index + 1}: {e}")
            print("ğŸ”„ Äá»•i sang API key tiáº¿p theo...")
            switch_key()

    # Náº¿u cháº¡y háº¿t vÃ²ng mÃ  táº¥t cáº£ key Ä‘á»u lá»—i
    raise Exception("âŒ Táº¥t cáº£ API key Ä‘á»u lá»—i hoáº·c háº¿t quota.")


# ==============================
# 5. CHáº Y QUA Tá»ªNG Cáº¢NH & LÆ¯U RA FILE
# ==============================

def main():
    if not scenes:
        print("âš ï¸ KhÃ´ng cÃ³ cáº£nh nÃ o trong scenes.txt â€“ kiá»ƒm tra láº¡i file input.")
        return

    with open(OUTPUT_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8") as out_f:
        for idx, scene in enumerate(scenes, start=1):
            print(f"â³ Äang xá»­ lÃ½ cáº£nh {idx}/{len(scenes)}...")

            # GhÃ©p cáº£nh vÃ o template
            full_prompt = PROMPT_TEMPLATE.replace("<<SCENE>>", scene)

            # Gá»i Gemini Ä‘á»ƒ sinh JSON 1 dÃ²ng
            json_line = call_gemini(full_prompt)

import json
import time
from google import generativeai as gen

# ================================
# 1. CONFIG
# ================================

API_KEYS = [
    "API_KEY_1",
    "API_KEY_2",
    "API_KEY_3"
    # thÃªm bao nhiÃªu cÅ©ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c
]

MODEL_NAME = "gemini-1.5-flash"      # Model báº¡n Ä‘ang dÃ¹ng
SCENES_FILE = "scenes.txt"           # File input cáº£nh
OUTPUT_FILE = "output_prompts.txt"   # File chá»©a prompt JSON

current_key_index = 0


# ================================
# 2. API KEY SWITCHING
# ================================

def set_current_key():
    gen.configure(api_key=API_KEYS[current_key_index])
    print(f"\nğŸ”‘ Äang dÃ¹ng API key #{current_key_index+1}")

def switch_key():
    global current_key_index
    current_key_index = (current_key_index + 1) % len(API_KEYS)
    set_current_key()

set_current_key()


# ================================
# 3. LOAD SCENES
# ================================

def load_scenes(path=SCENES_FILE):
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        content = f.read().strip()

    scenes = []
    chunks = content.split("Scene ")

    for c in chunks[1:]:
        num, rest = c.split(":", 1)
        scenes.append(f"Scene {num.strip()}: {rest.strip()}")

    return scenes


# ================================
# 4. SUPER PROMPT TEMPLATE
# ================================

PROMPT_TEMPLATE = """
Báº¡n lÃ  AI sinh JSON Ä‘iá»‡n áº£nh 1 dÃ²ng cho má»—i cáº£nh.

HÃ£y xuáº¥t Ä‘Ãºng cáº¥u trÃºc JSON sau (giá»¯ nguyÃªn Ä‘Ãºng field), KHÃ”NG giáº£i thÃ­ch thÃªm:

{
  "scene_number": {scene_number},
  "scene_title": "{scene_title}",
  "character": {{
    "name": "{character_name}",
    "appearance": "{character_appearance}",
    "emotions": {{
      "primary": "{emotion_primary}",
      "secondary": "{emotion_secondary}"
    }},
    "voice_tone": "{voice_tone}"
  }},
  "setting": {{
    "location": "{location}",
    "environment": "{environment}",
    "time": "{time_of_day}"
  }},
  "cinematic": {{
    "camera": "{camera}",
    "shot_type": "{shot_type}", 
    "primary_character": "{primary_character}",
    "lighting": "{lighting}",
    "mood": "{mood}",
    "style": "{style}",
    "effects": "{effects}",
    "sound": "{sound}"
  }},
  "dialogue": {{
    "characters": [
      {dialogue_block}
    ]
  }},
  "action_block": {{
    "length": "150-200 words",
    "content": "{action_content}"
  }}
}

LuÃ´n Ä‘áº£m báº£o:
- JSON há»£p lá»‡
- shot_type âˆˆ [CLOSEUP, EXTREME_CLOSEUP, MEDIUM, WIDE]
- primary_character âˆˆ [Alex, Maya, Marcus, None]
- Táº¥t cáº£ á»Ÿ 1 dÃ²ng.
"""


# ================================
# 5. AUTO RENAME FOR CLOSEUP
# ================================

def auto_rename(data):
    try:
        shot = data["cinematic"]["shot_type"]
        focus = data["cinematic"]["primary_character"]
    except:
        return data  # JSON lá»—i â†’ bá» qua

    # Báº£ng rename
    replace_map = {
        "Alex": "Alex2",
        "Maya": "Maya2",
        "Marcus": "Marcus2"
    }

    if shot in ["CLOSEUP", "EXTREME_CLOSEUP"]:
        if focus in replace_map:

            old = focus
            new = replace_map[focus]

            # Äá»•i character.name
            if data["character"]["name"] == old:
                data["character"]["name"] = new

            # Äá»•i primary_character
            data["cinematic"]["primary_character"] = new

            # Äá»•i dialogue speaker
            for d in data["dialogue"]["characters"]:
                if d["speaker"] == old:
                    d["speaker"] = new

            # Äá»•i trong action_block
            content = data["action_block"]["content"]
            content = content.replace(old, new)
            data["action_block"]["content"] = content

    return data


# ================================
# 6. CALL GEMINI
# ================================

def call_gemini(prompt):
    global current_key_index

    for _ in range(len(API_KEYS)):
        try:
            model = gen.GenerativeModel(MODEL_NAME)
            response = model.generate_content(prompt)
            text = response.text.strip()

            # Fix JSON lá»—i nhá»
            if text.startswith("```"):
                text = text.strip("```").strip()

            if not text.startswith("{"):
                raise ValueError("KhÃ´ng pháº£i JSON")

            data = json.loads(text)
            return data

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âš ï¸ Key #{current_key_index+1} lá»—i: {e}")
            switch_key()
            time.sleep(1)

    raise Exception("âŒ Táº¥t cáº£ API key Ä‘á»u lá»—i hoáº·c háº¿t quota!")


# ================================
# 7. MAIN PROCESS
# ================================

def main():
    scenes = load_scenes()
    print(f"\nğŸ“š ÄÃ£ náº¡p {len(scenes)} cáº£nh tá»« {SCENES_FILE}")

    output = open(OUTPUT_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8")

    for i, scene_text in enumerate(scenes):
        print(f"\nâ³ Xá»­ lÃ½ cáº£nh {i+1}/{len(scenes)}...")

        # ÄÃ¢y lÃ  prompt báº¡n gá»­i â†’ cho AI sinh JSON
        prompt = f"HÃ£y táº¡o JSON cho cáº£nh sau: {scene_text}"

        data = call_gemini(prompt)

        # Auto rename nhÃ¢n váº­t phiÃªn báº£n 2
        data = auto_rename(data)

        # Ghi xuá»‘ng file
        line = json.dumps(data, ensure_ascii=False)
        output.write(line + "\n")

        print(f"âœ… Xong cáº£nh {i+1}")

    output.close()
    print(f"\nğŸ‰ HOÃ€N Táº¤T! ÄÃ£ lÆ°u {len(scenes)} prompt vÃ o {OUTPUT_FILE}")


# ================================
# RUN
# ================================

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

ğŸ”§ Cáº­p nháº­t block cinematic (vá» máº·t thiáº¿t káº¿)

ğŸ”¹ Khi nÃ o kÃ­ch hoáº¡t Ä‘á»•i tÃªn?

Quy táº¯c: - shot_type âˆˆ ["CLOSEUP","EXTREME_CLOSEUP","MEDIUM","WIDE"]. - focus_characters lÃ  array, má»—i pháº§n tá»­ âˆˆ ["Alex","Maya","Marcus"], tá»‘i Ä‘a 3 pháº§n tá»­. - JSON pháº£i há»£p lá»‡, Ä‘Ãºng 1 dÃ²ng, khÃ´ng markdown, khÃ´ng giáº£i thÃ­ch thÃªm.
ğŸ“Œ GIáº¢I THÃCH NHANH (KHÃ”NG Cáº¦N LÆ¯U, CHá»ˆ Äá»‚ YÃŠN TÃ‚M)
â—¾ Táº¥t cáº£ chá»— <...> sáº½ Ä‘Æ°á»£c Python .format() thay báº±ng dá»¯ liá»‡u cáº£nh

(khÃ´ng cáº¯t bá»›t, khÃ´ng rÃºt gá»n, cháº¡y tháº³ng trÃªn Windows Terminal Ä‘Æ°á»£c).

âœ” Há»— trá»£ xoay vÃ²ng API key
âœ” Sinh prompt theo siÃªu cáº¥u trÃºc JSON má»›i
âœ” Gemini táº¡o shot_type + focus_characters
âœ” Python tá»± Ä‘á»•i tÃªn: Alex â†’ Alex2 (khi cáº­n cáº£nh)
âœ” Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng lÆ°u 1 prompt = 1 dÃ²ng vÃ o output_prompts.txt
âœ” KhÃ´ng cáº§n sá»­a gÃ¬ thÃªm, chá»‰ Ä‘áº·t API key + scenes.txt

ğŸ“Œ FILE: generate_prompts.py
(copy toÃ n bá»™, khÃ´ng sÃ³t dÃ²ng nÃ o)

import json
import os
import google.generativeai as gen

# ===============================================
# 1. CONFIG
# ===============================================

API_KEYS = [
    "YOUR_API_KEY_1",
    "YOUR_API_KEY_2",
    "YOUR_API_KEY_3"
]

MODEL_NAME = "gemini-1.5-flash"
SCENES_FILE = "scenes.txt"
OUTPUT_FILE = "output_prompts.txt"

current_key_index = 0


# ===============================================
# 2. API KEY HANDLING
# ===============================================

def set_current_key():
    gen.configure(api_key=API_KEYS[current_key_index])
    print(f"ğŸ”‘ Äang dÃ¹ng API key #{current_key_index+1}")

def switch_key():
    global current_key_index
    current_key_index = (current_key_index + 1) % len(API_KEYS)
    set_current_key()

set_current_key()


# ===============================================
# 3. LOAD SCENES (scene 1, scene 2â€¦)
# ===============================================

def load_scenes(path=SCENES_FILE):
    if not os.path.exists(path):
        print("âŒ KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y scenes.txt")
        return []

    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        text = f.read().strip()

    blocks = []
    raw = text.split("Scene ")
    for part in raw[1:]:
        num, rest = part.split(":", 1)
        num = num.strip()
        content = rest.strip()
        blocks.append((num, content))
    return blocks


scenes = load_scenes()
print(f"ğŸ“š ÄÃ£ náº¡p {len(scenes)} cáº£nh tá»« {SCENES_FILE}")


# ===============================================
# 4. SUPER PROMPT TEMPLATE (ONE-LINE JSON)
# ===============================================

SUPER_PROMPT = (
    'HÃ£y táº¡o JSON 1 dÃ²ng mÃ´ táº£ cáº£nh phim theo cáº¥u trÃºc sau, khÃ´ng giáº£i thÃ­ch: '
    '{{"scene_number":{scene_number},"scene_title":"{scene_title}",'
    '"character":{{"name":"Alex","appearance":"<auto>","emotions":{{"primary":"<auto>","secondary":"<auto>"}},'
    '"voice_tone":"<auto>"}},'
    '"setting":{{"location":"<auto>","environment":"<auto>","time":"<auto>"}},'
    '"cinematic":{{"camera":"<auto>","shot_type":"<auto>","focus_characters":<auto>,'
    '"lighting":"<auto>","mood":"<auto>","style":"Cinematic 8K realistic","effects":"<auto>","sound":"<auto>"}},'
    '"dialogue":{{"characters":<auto>}},'
    '"action_block":{{"length":"150-200 words","content":"<auto>"}}}} '
    'Quy táº¯c: shot_type âˆˆ ["CLOSEUP","EXTREME_CLOSEUP","MEDIUM","WIDE"]. '
    'focus_characters lÃ  array âˆˆ ["Alex","Maya","Marcus"], tá»‘i Ä‘a 3. '
    'JSON há»£p lá»‡, Ä‘Ãºng 1 dÃ²ng.'
)


# ===============================================
# 5. CALL GEMINI
# ===============================================

def call_gemini(prompt):
    for attempt in range(len(API_KEYS)):
        try:
            model = gen.GenerativeModel(MODEL_NAME)
            response = model.generate_content(prompt)
            return response.text.strip()

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âš ï¸ Key #{current_key_index+1} lá»—i: {e}")
            switch_key()

    raise Exception("âŒ Táº¥t cáº£ API key Ä‘á»u lá»—i hoáº·c háº¿t quota.")


# ===============================================
# 6. AUTO-RENAME (Close-up logic)
# ===============================================

def apply_closeup_renaming(json_data):
    shot = json_data["cinematic"].get("shot_type", "")
    focus = json_data["cinematic"].get("focus_characters", [])

    if shot not in ["CLOSEUP", "EXTREME_CLOSEUP"]:
        return json_data  # cáº£nh thÆ°á»ng â†’ giá»¯ nguyÃªn

    rename_map = {}
    for char in focus:
        rename_map[char] = char + "2"

    def replace_text(text):
        for old, new in rename_map.items():
            text = text.replace(old, new)
        return text

    # Character name
    name = json_data["character"]["name"]
    if name in rename_map:
        json_data["character"]["name"] = rename_map[name]

    # Focus list
    json_data["cinematic"]["focus_characters"] = [
        rename_map.get(x, x) for x in focus
    ]

    # Dialogue
    for block in json_data["dialogue"]["characters"]:
        sp = block["speaker"]
        if sp in rename_map:
            block["speaker"] = rename_map[sp]
        block["line"] = replace_text(block["line"])

    # Action text
    json_data["action_block"]["content"] = replace_text(json_data["action_block"]["content"])

    return json_data


# ===============================================
# 7. MAIN
# ===============================================

def main():
    if len(scenes) == 0:
        print("âŒ KhÃ´ng cÃ³ cáº£nh nÃ o Ä‘á»ƒ xá»­ lÃ½.")
        return

    output = []

    for idx, (scene_number, scene_text) in enumerate(scenes, 1):
        print(f"â³ Äang xá»­ lÃ½ cáº£nh {idx}/{len(scenes)}...")

        prompt = SUPER_PROMPT.format(
            scene_number=scene_number,
            scene_title=scene_text.replace('"', "'")
        )

        raw_response = call_gemini(prompt)

        try:
            json_data = json.loads(raw_response)
        except:
            print("âŒ Gemini tráº£ JSON lá»—i â†’ bá» qua cáº£nh nÃ y.")
            continue

        json_data = apply_closeup_renaming(json_data)

        output.append(json.dumps(json_data, ensure_ascii=False))

    with open(OUTPUT_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for line in output:
            f.write(line + "\n")

    print(f"\nâœ… Xong! ÄÃ£ lÆ°u {len(output)} prompt vÃ o {OUTPUT_FILE}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

def apply_character_definitions(data):
    name = data["character"]["name"]  # Alex, Maya, Marcus hoáº·c Alex2 (close-up)
    
    # Bá» â€œ2â€ náº¿u lÃ  báº£n close-up
    base_name = name[:-1] if name.endswith("2") else name

    if base_name in CHAR_DEFS:
        data["character"]["appearance"] = CHAR_DEFS[base_name]
    
    return data
NhÆ° váº­y:

Káº¿t quáº£:

Python chá»‰ cáº§n:

Xem trong JSON cáº£nh nÃ y cÃ³ Alex / Maya / Marcus khÃ´ng (tÃªn trong focus_characters, dialogue, character.name)

(TÃ´i sáº½ chá»‰ táº­p trung vÃ o code, khÃ´ng viáº¿t máº«u ná»™i dung prompt dÃ i dÃ²ng nhÆ° báº¡n dáº·n.)

ğŸ“ Node 3: build_final_prompts.py
Chá»©c nÄƒng:

Äá»c tá»«ng dÃ²ng JSON tá»« output_prompts.txt (Node 2 Ä‘Ã£ táº¡o).

Dá»±a vÃ o Ä‘Ã³, ghÃ©p thÃªm Ä‘á»‹nh nghÄ©a nhÃ¢n váº­t lÃªn Ä‘áº§u prompt.

Xuáº¥t ra file final_prompts.txt, má»—i cáº£nh = 1 dÃ²ng prompt text.

Báº¡n chá»‰ cáº§n tá»± Ä‘iá»n mÃ´ táº£ nhÃ¢n váº­t vÃ o CHAR_DEFS, cÃ²n láº¡i Python lo.

ğŸ”§ Code FULL 100% (copy nguyÃªn vÃ o file build_final_prompts.py)
import json
import os

# =====================================
# 1. Äá»ŠNH NGHÄ¨A NHÃ‚N Váº¬T Cá» Äá»ŠNH
# =====================================
# ğŸ‘‰ Báº¡n Tá»° ÄIá»€N mÃ´ táº£ á»Ÿ Ä‘Ã¢y. KhÃ´ng cáº§n sá»­a code bÃªn dÆ°á»›i.

CHAR_DEFS = {
    "Alex":   "Alex: (Ä‘iá»n mÃ´ táº£ cá»‘ Ä‘á»‹nh á»Ÿ Ä‘Ã¢y).",
    "Maya":   "Maya: (Ä‘iá»n mÃ´ táº£ cá»‘ Ä‘á»‹nh á»Ÿ Ä‘Ã¢y).",
    "Marcus": "Marcus: (Ä‘iá»n mÃ´ táº£ cá»‘ Ä‘á»‹nh á»Ÿ Ä‘Ã¢y)."
}

INPUT_JSON_FILE = "output_prompts.txt"   # file tá»« Node 2
OUTPUT_PROMPT_FILE = "final_prompts.txt" # file prompt cuá»‘i cÃ¹ng


# =====================================
# 2. HÃ€M Láº¤Y TÃŠN Gá»C (Xá»¬ LÃ Alex2 â†’ Alex)
# =====================================

def base_name(name: str) -> str:
    """
    Alex2 -> Alex
    Maya2 -> Maya
    Marcus2 -> Marcus
    CÃ¡c tÃªn khÃ¡c giá»¯ nguyÃªn.
    """
    if name.endswith("2") and len(name) > 1:
        return name[:-1]
    return name


# =====================================
# 3. TÃŒM NHÃ‚N Váº¬T CÃ“ Máº¶T TRONG Cáº¢NH
# =====================================

def detect_characters(scene_json: dict) -> list:
    """
    Tráº£ vá» danh sÃ¡ch tÃªn nhÃ¢n váº­t XUáº¤T HIá»†N trong cáº£nh,
    dáº¡ng phiÃªn báº£n hiá»‡n táº¡i (Alex / Alex2 / Maya / Maya2...),
    KHÃ”NG trÃ¹ng láº·p, giá»¯ thá»© tá»± xuáº¥t hiá»‡n.
    """
    found = []

    # 1) character.name
    char_name = scene_json.get("character", {}).get("name", "")
    if char_name:
        found.append(char_name)

    # 2) cinematic.focus_characters (list)
    focus_list = scene_json.get("cinematic", {}).get("focus_characters", [])
    if isinstance(focus_list, list):
        for n in focus_list:
            if n and n not in found:
                found.append(n)

    # 3) dialogue.characters[].speaker
    dialogue = scene_json.get("dialogue", {}).get("characters", [])
    if isinstance(dialogue, list):
        for d in dialogue:
            sp = d.get("speaker", "")
            if sp and sp not in found:
                found.append(sp)

    return found


# =====================================
# 4. GHÃ‰P Äá»ŠNH NGHÄ¨A NHÃ‚N Váº¬T + Ná»˜I DUNG Cáº¢NH
# =====================================

def build_prompt_line(scene_json: dict) -> str:
    """
    Táº¡o 1 dÃ²ng prompt text hoÃ n chá»‰nh tá»« JSON cáº£nh:
    - Pháº§n Ä‘áº§u: Ä‘á»‹nh nghÄ©a nhÃ¢n váº­t (náº¿u cÃ³ trong cáº£nh)
    - Pháº§n sau: action_block.content (Ä‘Ã£ bá» xuá»‘ng dÃ²ng)
    ğŸ‘‰ Káº¿t quáº£ tráº£ vá»: 1 string, khÃ´ng xuá»‘ng dÃ²ng.
    """

    # 4.1. TÃ¬m cÃ¡c nhÃ¢n váº­t xuáº¥t hiá»‡n
    present = detect_characters(scene_json)  # vÃ­ dá»¥: ["Alex2", "Maya"]

    # 4.2. Táº¡o block Ä‘á»‹nh nghÄ©a nhÃ¢n váº­t
    def_parts = []
    for name in present:
        base = base_name(name)
        if base in CHAR_DEFS and CHAR_DEFS[base].strip():
            # VÃ­ dá»¥: "Alex2: [mÃ´ táº£ Alex]"
            def_parts.append(f"{name}: {CHAR_DEFS[base]}")

    # 4.3. Láº¥y pháº§n hÃ nh Ä‘á»™ng chÃ­nh cá»§a cáº£nh
    action_text = scene_json.get("action_block", {}).get("content", "")
    # Bá» xuá»‘ng dÃ²ng cho gá»n 1 dÃ²ng
    action_text = " ".join(action_text.split())

    # 4.4. GhÃ©p láº¡i thÃ nh 1 dÃ²ng
    # Náº¿u cÃ³ Ä‘á»‹nh nghÄ©a nhÃ¢n váº­t -> [defs] || [action]
    # Náº¿u khÃ´ng -> chá»‰ láº¥y action
    if def_parts:
        defs_section = " | ".join(def_parts)
        full_prompt = f"{defs_section} || {action_text}"
    else:
        full_prompt = action_text

    return full_prompt.strip()


# =====================================
# 5. MAIN: Äá»ŒC JSON LINES â†’ XUáº¤T FINAL PROMPTS
# =====================================

def main():
    if not os.path.exists(INPUT_JSON_FILE):
        print(f"âŒ KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y file {INPUT_JSON_FILE}")
        return

    final_lines = []
    total = 0

    with open(INPUT_JSON_FILE, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for line in f:
            line = line.strip()
            if not line:
                continue

            try:
                scene_json = json.loads(line)
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"âš ï¸ Bá» qua 1 dÃ²ng JSON lá»—i: {e}")
                continue

            prompt_line = build_prompt_line(scene_json)
            final_lines.append(prompt_line)
            total += 1

    with open(OUTPUT_PROMPT_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for p in final_lines:
            f.write(p + "\n")

    print(f"âœ… ÄÃ£ táº¡o {total} prompt vÃ o file: {OUTPUT_PROMPT_FILE}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
ğŸ§© CÃ¡ch dÃ¹ng nhanh
Äáº£m báº£o báº¡n Ä‘Ã£ cÃ³ file:

output_prompts.txt (Node 2 Ä‘Ã£ táº¡o, má»—i dÃ²ng lÃ  1 JSON cáº£nh)

    "Alex":   "Alex: 36 tuá»•i, tÃ³c ngáº¯n nÃ¢u, cÆ¡ báº¯p. ...",

}
Cháº¡y trong thÆ° má»¥c Ä‘Ã³:

File final_prompts.txt

Má»—i dÃ²ng = 1 prompt gá»“m:

||

Ná»™i dung hÃ nh Ä‘á»™ng cá»§a cáº£nh (action_block.content)

Náº¿u sau nÃ y báº¡n muá»‘n:

ThÃªm language tag (e.g. â€œEnglish prompt:â€ / â€œVietnamese prompt:â€)

Hoáº·c thÃªm pháº§n setting + cinematic.camera vÃ o cuá»‘i prompt

â†’ chá»‰ cáº§n sá»­a nháº¹ trong hÃ m build_prompt_line().
Khi cáº§n, nÃ³i: â€œSá»­a Node 3 thÃªm setting + cameraâ€ lÃ  mÃ¬nh lÃ m tiáº¿p.

Báº¡n Ä‘Ã£ nÃ³i:
Sá»­a Node 3 thÃªm setting + camera vÃ  ThÃªm language tag (e.g. â€œEnglish prompt:â€ / â€œVietnamese prompt:â€)
ChatGPT Ä‘Ã£ nÃ³i:
DÆ°á»›i Ä‘Ã¢y lÃ  Node 3 phiÃªn báº£n nÃ¢ng cáº¥p FULL, theo yÃªu cáº§u má»›i cá»§a báº¡n:

âœ” ThÃªm ngÃ´n ngá»¯ Ä‘áº§u ra:
English prompt: hoáº·c

Vietnamese prompt:
â†’ báº¡n chá»‰ cáº§n chá»‰nh 1 biáº¿n duy nháº¥t: LANGUAGE_TAG

âœ” ThÃªm SETTING vÃ o prompt cuá»‘i
â†’ (Location + Environment + Time)

âœ” ThÃªm CAMERA
â†’ (camera + shot_type)

âœ” Cáº¥u trÃºc final prompt =
[language_tag] [Character Definitions] || [SETTING] || [CAMERA] || [ACTION]
ğŸš€ FILE HOÃ€N CHá»ˆNH: build_final_prompts.py (Version 2 â€“ PRO)
(copy toÃ n bá»™, khÃ´ng bá» dÃ²ng nÃ o)

import json
import os

# =====================================
# 1. Äá»ŠNH NGHÄ¨A NHÃ‚N Váº¬T Cá» Äá»ŠNH
# =====================================
# ğŸ‘‰ Báº¡n tá»± Ä‘iá»n mÃ´ táº£ á»Ÿ Ä‘Ã¢y (khÃ´ng sá»­a code).
CHAR_DEFS = {
    "Alex":   "Alex: (Ä‘iá»n mÃ´ táº£ cá»‘ Ä‘á»‹nh á»Ÿ Ä‘Ã¢y).",
    "Maya":   "Maya: (Ä‘iá»n mÃ´ táº£ cá»‘ Ä‘á»‹nh á»Ÿ Ä‘Ã¢y).",
    "Marcus": "Marcus: (Ä‘iá»n mÃ´ táº£ cá»‘ Ä‘á»‹nh á»Ÿ Ä‘Ã¢y)."
}

# Chá»n gáº¯n tag ngÃ´n ngá»¯
# LANGUAGE_TAG = "English prompt:"
LANGUAGE_TAG = "Vietnamese prompt:"

INPUT_JSON_FILE = "output_prompts.txt"
OUTPUT_PROMPT_FILE = "final_prompts.txt"


# =====================================
# 2. CHUYá»‚N Alex2 â†’ Alex (base name)
# =====================================

def base_name(name: str) -> str:
    if name.endswith("2") and len(name) > 1:
        return name[:-1]
    return name


# =====================================
# 3. TÃŒM NHÃ‚N Váº¬T XUáº¤T HIá»†N TRONG Cáº¢NH
# =====================================

def detect_characters(scene_json: dict) -> list:
    found = []

    # A) character.name
    char_name = scene_json.get("character", {}).get("name", "")
    if char_name:
        found.append(char_name)

    # B) cinematic.focus_characters
    focus_list = scene_json.get("cinematic", {}).get("focus_characters", [])
    if isinstance(focus_list, list):
        for n in focus_list:
            if n and n not in found:
                found.append(n)

    # C) dialogue speakers
    dialogue = scene_json.get("dialogue", {}).get("characters", [])
    if isinstance(dialogue, list):
        for d in dialogue:
            sp = d.get("speaker", "")
            if sp and sp not in found:
                found.append(sp)

    return found


# =====================================
# 4. GHÃ‰P PROMPT FINAL
# =====================================

def build_prompt_line(scene_json: dict) -> str:

    # -----------------------
    # 4.1. Character definitions
    # -----------------------
    present = detect_characters(scene_json)

    def_parts = []
    for name in present:
        bname = base_name(name)
        if bname in CHAR_DEFS and CHAR_DEFS[bname].strip():
            def_parts.append(f"{name}: {CHAR_DEFS[bname]}")

    defs_section = " | ".join(def_parts) if def_parts else ""


    # -----------------------
    # 4.2. SETTING
    # -----------------------
    st = scene_json.get("setting", {})
    loc = st.get("location", "")
    env = st.get("environment", "")
    time = st.get("time", "")

    setting_section = f"Setting: {loc}. {env}. Time: {time}."
    setting_section = " ".join(setting_section.split())


    # -----------------------
    # 4.3. CAMERA
    # -----------------------
    cine = scene_json.get("cinematic", {})
    cam = cine.get("camera", "")
    shot = cine.get("shot_type", "")

    camera_section = f"Camera: {cam}. Shot Type: {shot}."
    camera_section = " ".join(camera_section.split())


    # -----------------------
    # 4.4. ACTION
    # -----------------------
    action_text = scene_json.get("action_block", {}).get("content", "")
    action_text = " ".join(action_text.split())


    # -----------------------
    # 4.5. FINAL LINE FORMAT
    # -----------------------
    # [LANG] [Defs] || [Setting] || [Camera] || [Action]
    parts = [LANGUAGE_TAG]

    if defs_section:
        parts.append(defs_section)

    parts.append(setting_section)
    parts.append(camera_section)
    parts.append(action_text)

    return " || ".join(parts).strip()


# =====================================
# 5. MAIN
# =====================================

def main():
    if not os.path.exists(INPUT_JSON_FILE):
        print(f"âŒ KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y file {INPUT_JSON_FILE}")
        return

    final_lines = []
    count = 0

    with open(INPUT_JSON_FILE, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for line in f:
            line = line.strip()
            if not line:
                continue

            try:
                scene_json = json.loads(line)
            except:
                print("âš ï¸ JSON lá»—i â†’ bá» qua")
                continue

            final_line = build_prompt_line(scene_json)
            final_lines.append(final_line)
            count += 1

    with open(OUTPUT_PROMPT_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for p in final_lines:
            f.write(p + "\n")

    print(f"âœ… ÄÃ£ xuáº¥t {count} prompt vÃ o {OUTPUT_PROMPT_FILE}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

ğŸ‘‰ ÄÃ¢y lÃ  cÃ¡ch tá»‘t nháº¥t Ä‘á»ƒ táº¡o video vÃ¬:

Báº£n tiáº¿ng Anh: dÃ¹ng cho AI video

â¡ Xuáº¥t 2 file:

final_prompts_en.txt â€“ prompt tiáº¿ng Anh

final_prompts_vi.txt â€“ báº£n dá»‹ch tiáº¿ng Viá»‡t (AI dá»‹ch, giá»¯ nguyÃªn ||)

DÆ°á»›i Ä‘Ã¢y lÃ  file hoÃ n chá»‰nh build_final_prompts.py (báº£n má»›i, thay tháº¿ báº£n cÅ©):

import json
import os
import google.generativeai as gen

# =====================================
# 1. CONFIG
# =====================================

# ğŸ‘‰ Báº¡n Tá»° ÄIá»€N mÃ´ táº£ nhÃ¢n váº­t báº±ng TIáº¾NG ANH (vÃ¬ prompt gá»‘c lÃ  English)
CHAR_DEFS = {
    "Alex":   "Alex: 36 years old, short brown hair, muscular build, wearing a black leather jacket, cargo pants and hiking boots. Wears a wide gray brimmed hat, scar on the left cheek, tough leader aura.",
    "Maya":   "Maya: (fill fixed English description here).",
    "Marcus": "Marcus: (fill fixed English description here)."
}

INPUT_JSON_FILE = "output_prompts.txt"
OUTPUT_PROMPT_EN_FILE = "final_prompts_en.txt"
OUTPUT_PROMPT_VI_FILE = "final_prompts_vi.txt"

# API KEY LIST (dÃ¹ng láº¡i style xoay key nhÆ° Node 2)
API_KEYS = [
    "YOUR_API_KEY_1",
    "YOUR_API_KEY_2"
    # thÃªm náº¿u muá»‘n
]

MODEL_NAME = "gemini-1.5-flash"
current_key_index = 0


# =====================================
# 2. GEMINI CONFIG + KEY SWITCH
# =====================================

def set_current_key():
    gen.configure(api_key=API_KEYS[current_key_index])
    print(f"ğŸ”‘ Node3: Äang dÃ¹ng API key #{current_key_index+1}")

def switch_key():
    global current_key_index
    current_key_index = (current_key_index + 1) % len(API_KEYS)
    set_current_key()

set_current_key()


# =====================================
# 3. HÃ€M CHUNG
# =====================================

def base_name(name: str) -> str:
    """Alex2 -> Alex, Maya2 -> Maya, Marcus2 -> Marcus."""
    if name.endswith("2") and len(name) > 1:
        return name[:-1]
    return name


def detect_characters(scene_json: dict) -> list:
    """Tráº£ vá» danh sÃ¡ch tÃªn nhÃ¢n váº­t xuáº¥t hiá»‡n trong cáº£nh (Alex, Alex2, Maya...)."""
    found = []

    # A) character.name
    char_name = scene_json.get("character", {}).get("name", "")
    if char_name:
        found.append(char_name)

    # B) cinematic.focus_characters
    focus_list = scene_json.get("cinematic", {}).get("focus_characters", [])
    if isinstance(focus_list, list):
        for n in focus_list:
            if n and n not in found:
                found.append(n)

    # C) dialogue speakers
    dialogue = scene_json.get("dialogue", {}).get("characters", [])
    if isinstance(dialogue, list):
        for d in dialogue:
            sp = d.get("speaker", "")
            if sp and sp not in found:
                found.append(sp)

    return found


# =====================================
# 4. BUILD ENGLISH PROMPT LINE
# =====================================

def build_prompt_line_en(scene_json: dict) -> str:
    """
    Format final EN:
    English prompt: [CharDefs] || [Setting] || [Camera] || [Action]
    """

    # 4.1 Character defs
    present = detect_characters(scene_json)
    def_parts = []

    for name in present:
        bname = base_name(name)
        if bname in CHAR_DEFS and CHAR_DEFS[bname].strip():
            def_parts.append(f"{name}: {CHAR_DEFS[bname]}")

    defs_section = " | ".join(def_parts) if def_parts else ""

    # 4.2 Setting
    st = scene_json.get("setting", {})
    loc = st.get("location", "")
    env = st.get("environment", "")
    time = st.get("time", "")

    setting_section = f"Setting: {loc}. {env}. Time: {time}."
    setting_section = " ".join(setting_section.split())

    # 4.3 Camera
    cine = scene_json.get("cinematic", {})
    cam = cine.get("camera", "")
    shot = cine.get("shot_type", "")

    camera_section = f"Camera: {cam}. Shot Type: {shot}."
    camera_section = " ".join(camera_section.split())

    # 4.4 Action
    action_text = scene_json.get("action_block", {}).get("content", "")
    action_text = " ".join(action_text.split())

    # 4.5 Join
    parts = ["English prompt:"]

    if defs_section:
        parts.append(defs_section)

    parts.append(setting_section)
    parts.append(camera_section)
    parts.append(action_text)

    return " || ".join(parts).strip()


# =====================================
# 5. TRANSLATE EN â†’ VI USING GEMINI
# =====================================

def translate_to_vi(text_en: str) -> str:
    """
    Dá»‹ch 1 dÃ²ng prompt tiáº¿ng Anh sang tiáº¿ng Viá»‡t,
    giá»¯ nguyÃªn 'English prompt:' -> Ä‘á»•i thÃ nh 'Vietnamese prompt:',
    giá»¯ nguyÃªn cáº¥u trÃºc '||'.
    """
    # Ä‘á»•i tag trÆ°á»›c cho cháº¯c
    if text_en.startswith("English prompt:"):
        base = text_en[len("English prompt:"):].lstrip()
        text_en_clean = base
    else:
        text_en_clean = text_en

    prompt = (
        "Dá»‹ch nguyÃªn vÄƒn Ä‘oáº¡n sau sang tiáº¿ng Viá»‡t, giá»¯ nguyÃªn cáº¥u trÃºc phÃ¢n tÃ¡ch báº±ng '||', "
        "khÃ´ng thÃªm giáº£i thÃ­ch, khÃ´ng thÃªm cÃ¢u má»›i, chá»‰ dá»‹ch ná»™i dung. "
        "KhÃ´ng dá»‹ch tÃªn riÃªng Alex, Maya, Marcus, Alex2, Maya2, Marcus2.\n\n"
        f"{text_en_clean}"
    )

    for _ in range(len(API_KEYS)):
        try:
            model = gen.GenerativeModel(MODEL_NAME)
            resp = model.generate_content(prompt)
            text_vi = resp.text.strip()
            # gom vá» 1 dÃ²ng
            text_vi = " ".join(text_vi.split())
            return f"Vietnamese prompt: {text_vi}"
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âš ï¸ Lá»—i dá»‹ch sang VI vá»›i key #{current_key_index+1}: {e}")
            switch_key()

    # náº¿u táº¥t cáº£ key lá»—i â†’ fallback: dÃ¹ng tiáº¿ng Anh, Ä‘á»•i tag Ä‘á»ƒ dá»… nháº­n
    print("âŒ KhÃ´ng dá»‹ch Ä‘Æ°á»£c sang tiáº¿ng Viá»‡t, dÃ¹ng táº¡m báº£n EN.")
    return "Vietnamese prompt (fallback EN): " + text_en_clean


# =====================================
# 6. MAIN: READ JSON LINES â†’ 2 FILE
# =====================================

def main():
    if not os.path.exists(INPUT_JSON_FILE):
        print(f"âŒ KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y file {INPUT_JSON_FILE}")
        return

    en_lines = []
    vi_lines = []
    count = 0

    with open(INPUT_JSON_FILE, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for line in f:
            line = line.strip()
            if not line:
                continue

            try:
                scene_json = json.loads(line)
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"âš ï¸ JSON lá»—i, bá» qua 1 dÃ²ng: {e}")
                continue

            # Build EN line
            line_en = build_prompt_line_en(scene_json)
            en_lines.append(line_en)

            # Translate to VI
            line_vi = translate_to_vi(line_en)
            vi_lines.append(line_vi)

            count += 1
            print(f"âœ… ÄÃ£ xá»­ lÃ½ cáº£nh #{count}")

    # Ghi file EN
    with open(OUTPUT_PROMPT_EN_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for p in en_lines:
            f.write(p + "\n")

    # Ghi file VI
    with open(OUTPUT_PROMPT_VI_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for p in vi_lines:
            f.write(p + "\n")

    print(f"\nğŸ‰ HOÃ€N Táº¤T! ÄÃ£ xuáº¥t {count} prompt EN â†’ {OUTPUT_PROMPT_EN_FILE}")
    print(f"ğŸ‰ HOÃ€N Táº¤T! ÄÃ£ xuáº¥t {count} prompt VI â†’ {OUTPUT_PROMPT_VI_FILE}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
